.9-.4.9-.9v-10.2c0-.5-.4-.9-.9-.9H16a.5.5 0 0 1 0-1" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg><div class="j i d"><p class="bf b bg z du">Share</p></div></button></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><h1 id="389d" class="mq mr gv bf ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm nn bk">Translation of the CERT-UA#9474 &amp; Threat Hunting Opportunities</h1><p id="4ebe" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh oi oj ok ol go bk">This is the translation of the CERT-UA#9474 with some additional information and hunting opportunities.</p><h2 id="46ca" class="om mr gv bf ms on oo dy mw op oq ea na nz or os ot od ou ov ow oh ox oy oz pa bk">General Information</h2><p id="741b" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh oi oj ok ol go bk pb"><span class="l pc pd pe bo pf pg ph pi pj fj">T</span>he government computer emergency response team of Ukraine CERT-UA takes organizational and technical measures to prevent, detect and respond to cyber incidents and cyber attacks.</p><p id="07d2" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr pk nt nu nv pl nx ny nz pm ob oc od pn of og oh po oj ok ol go bk">Therefore, during 2024, the increased activity of the UAC-0184 group is recorded, which aims to gain access to the computers of representatives of the Defense Forces of Ukraine in order to steal documents and messenger data.</p><p id="2c18" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr pk nt nu nv pl nx ny nz pm ob oc od pn of og oh po oj ok ol go bk">As a rule, the main channel for the <strong class="nq gw">delivery of malware is popular messengers</strong>, and the methods of initial infiltration involve the use of elements of s<strong class="nq gw">ocial engineering</strong>, among which, for example, an accompanying message-bait on the topic of the opening of an executive/criminal case, a video of combat operations, or a request for acquaintance through popular platforms and subsequent correspondence with a serviceman, during which a file (archive) is transferred to the latter with a request for help in opening/processing it.</p><p id="eedb" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr pk nt nu nv pl nx ny nz pm ob oc od pn of og oh po oj ok ol go bk">In the process of implementing a malicious plan, attackers use a certain set of software, including both commercial programs and open source utilities, in particular:</p><p id="524e" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr pk nt nu nv pl nx ny nz pm ob oc od pn of og oh po oj ok ol go bk">• <strong class="nq gw">IDAT </strong>(HijackLoader, SHADOWLADDER, GHOSTPULSE); used at the stage of primary damage</p><p id="6704" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr pk nt nu nv pl nx ny nz pm ob oc od pn of og oh po oj ok ol go bk">• <strong class="nq gw">REMCOSRAT</strong></p><p id="6576" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr pk nt nu nv pl nx ny nz pm ob oc od pn of og oh po oj ok ol go bk">• <strong class="nq gw">VIOTTOKEYLOGGER</strong></p><p id="a5d1" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr pk nt nu nv pl nx ny nz pm ob oc od pn of og oh po oj ok ol go bk">• <strong class="nq gw">XWORM</strong></p><p id="d68b" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr pk nt nu nv pl nx ny nz pm ob oc od pn of og oh po oj ok ol go bk">• <strong class="nq gw">SIGTOP</strong> (hxxps://github[.]com/tbvdm/sigtop)</p><p id="8096" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr pk nt nu nv pl nx ny nz pm ob oc od pn of og oh po oj ok ol go bk">• <strong class="nq gw">TUSC</strong> (hxxps://github[.]com/jackhftang/tusc)</p><p id="027d" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr pk nt nu nv pl nx ny nz pm ob oc od pn of og oh po oj ok ol go bk">At the same time, <strong class="nq gw">SIGTOP</strong> and <strong class="nq gw">TUSC</strong> are used to steal and download data from computers, in particular, messages and contact data of <strong class="nq gw">Signal</strong>, which is quite popular among the military.</p><p id="12d6" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr pk nt nu nv pl nx ny nz pm ob oc od pn of og oh po oj ok ol go bk pb"><span class="l pc pd pe bo pf pg ph pi pj fj">We</span> draw your attention and ask you to understand the fact that attackers will improve the methods of delivering malicious programs using popular messengers, which, from the point of view of software protection tools, are an insufficiently controlled channel of information exchange. At the same time, any careless online activity of a serviceman (for example, posting a photo in military uniform) makes it easier for attackers to identify priority targets for attacks.</p><p id="aa0c" class="pw-post-body-paragraph no np gv nq b nr pk nt nu nv pl nx ny nz pm ob oc od pn of og oh po oj ok ol go bk">If you find any suspicious messages or files, please immediately inform CERT-UA and/or the ITS Cyber Security Center (unit A0334; email: csoc@post[.]mil[.]gov[.]ua, Signal: +380673321891).</p><h2 id="e2b5" class="om mr gv bf ms on oo dy mw op oq ea na nz or os ot od ou ov ow oh ox oy oz pa bk">Indicators of Cyber Threats</h2><figure class="ps pt pu pv pw px pp pq paragraph-image"><div role="button" tabindex="0" class="py pz fj qa bh qb"><div class="pp pq
